景德镇以盛产瓷器著称。
China is the common name for ware made of porcelain, given because it came from China.
瓷器是瓷质器皿的通用名称，取这个与中国书写相同的名称，是因为瓷器源于中国。
Porcelain, often called china or chinaware, is a type of ceramics highly valued for its beauty and strength.
瓷器，又称陶瓷或陶瓷器，是陶瓷制品的一种，因其外观美、强度高，所以价值不菲。
China, also known as soft-paste or tender porcelain, is softer: it can be cut with a file, while porcelain cannot.
陶器，也叫幼陶器或软瓷器，它的质地柔软，可以用锉刀切开，但是普通瓷器就不行。
Although porcelain is frequently used as a synonym for china, the two are not identical.
虽然瓷器常常被当作陶瓷的同义词，但两者并不完全相同。
a bombé china cabinet
凸起的瓷器柜
a china cabinet
瓷器(陈列)橱
her good china
她的上等瓷器
My wife only use the best china when we have visitors.
家里来客人的时候，妻子才会拿出最好的瓷器。
Spode china featured a large number of designs but was especially noted for its exotic birds.
斯波德瓷器有多种设计，但其最著名的是极具异国情调的鸟类设计。
Whereas porcelain is always translucent, china is opaque.
瓷器常常是半透明的，而陶器是不透明的。
Because it is easier to make, harder to chip, and stronger than hard porcelain, bone china has become the most popular type of porcelain in some countries.
骨瓷制作工艺简单，强度高，较之硬瓷更不易摔碎，所以在很多国家骨瓷是最受欢迎的瓷器。
This porcelain dinner service set is an antique.
这套瓷器餐具是古董。
Please handle china with care. It\'s fragile.
瓷器易碎，请轻拿轻放。
Please take a look at my most recent acquistion, an antique vase from the Qing dynasty.

请看看我最近得到的东西，这是一件清朝古瓷器。
The museum was showing a group of porcelain and wood sculpture crafted by European artisans.

这个博物馆正在展出一组由欧洲工匠制作的瓷器和木制雕塑。

Porcelain, often called china or chinaware, is a type of ceramics highly valued for its beauty and strength.
瓷器，又称陶瓷或陶瓷器，是陶瓷制品的一种，因其外观美、强度高，所以价值不菲。
Because it is easier to make, harder to chip, and stronger than hard porcelain, bone china has become the most popular type of porcelain in some countries.
骨瓷制作工艺简单，强度高，较之硬瓷更不易摔碎，所以在很多国家骨瓷是最受欢迎的瓷器。
China is the common name for ware made of porcelain, given because it came from China.
瓷器是瓷质器皿的通用名称，取这个与中国书写相同的名称，是因为瓷器源于中国。
This bone china tea set is decorated with bands of cornucopias with corn in them in gilt with some red enamel.
这套骨瓷茶具，杯边有象征富饶的羊角装饰，有镀金的谷物点缀，还刷了一层红瓷漆。
Although porcelain is frequently used as a synonym for china, the two are not identical.
虽然瓷器常常被当作陶瓷的同义词，但两者并不完全相同。
China, also known as soft-paste or tender porcelain, is softer: it can be cut with a file, while porcelain cannot.
陶器，也叫幼陶器或软瓷器，它的质地柔软，可以用锉刀切开，但是普通瓷器就不行。

Zuìzhōng，wǒmen zhǎodàole nénggòu tìhuàn nàxiē chéncílàndiào de yǔjù。
最终，我们找到了能够替换那些陈词滥调的语句。
&quot;It was a dark and stormy night&quot; is a hackneyed beginning for a story.
“Zhè shì gè yuèhēifēnggāo de yèwǎn”shì yí gè chéncílàndiào shì de gùshi kāichǎngbái。
“这是个月黑风高的夜晚”是一个陈词滥调式的故事开场白。
对于材木的砍伐要有计划，切不可盲目的滥砍滥伐。
Duìyú cáimù de kǎnfá yào yǒu jìhuà，qiè bùkě mángmù de lànkǎn lànfá。
Trees should be cut in a planned way instead of randomly.
长期的滥砍滥伐会造成严重的地质灾害。
Chángqī de lànkǎn lànfá huì zàochéng yánzhòng de dìzhì zāihài。
Illegal felling of trees for a long time will cause serious geological disasters.
滥捕滥杀野生鸟类是违法行为！
Lànbǔ lànshā yěshēng niǎolèi shì wéifǎ xíngwéi！
Excessive capturing and slaughtering of wild birds constitutes unlawful behavior.
河水泛滥。
Héshuǐ fànlàn。
The river was flooding. or The river overflowed its banks.
不能让错误思想自由泛滥。
Bùnéng ràng cuòwù sīxiǎng zìyóu fànlàn。
Under no circumstances should erroneous ideas be allowed to spread unchecked.
江水决堤，泛滥成灾。
Jiāngshuǐ juédī, fànlànchéngzāi。
The river overflowed its banks and caused serious flooding.
表格之多，闹得泛滥成灾。
Biǎogé zhī duō，nào de fànlànchéngzāi。
There is such a flood of statistical forms that they become a scourge.
滥施轰炸
làn shī hōngzhà
indiscriminate bombing; wanton bombing
滥发钞票
làn fā chāopiào
issue banknotes recklessly; inflate the paper currency
滥发奖金
làn fā jiǎngjīn
distribute bonuses indiscriminately
滥用经费
lànyòngjīngfèi
squander funds
不要滥用成语典故。
Búyào lànyòng chéngyǔ diǎngù。
We should not use proverbs and allusions indiscriminately.
巧立名目滥发奖金
qiǎolìmíngmù lànfā jiǎngjīn
invent excuses to give out extravagant bonuses
任其泛滥
rèn qí fànlàn
let it (e.g. a flood, etc.) spread unchecked
宁可虚位以待，也不要让不称职的人滥竽充数。
Nìngkě xūwèiyǐdài，yě búyào ràng bú chènzhí de rén lànyúchōngshù。
We\'d rather leave the place vacant than have someone incompetent fill the position.
滥竽充数
lànyúchōngshù
pass oneself off as one of the players in an ensemble—be there just to make up the number (used of incompetent people or inferior goods)
你不能因为睡眠不好就滥用安眠药。
Nǐ bùnéng yīnwèi shuìmián bùhǎo jiù lànyòng ānmiányào。
Because you have difficulty sleeping it doesn\'t mean you can overdose on sleeping pills.
健康的人不要滥用保健品。
Jiànkāng de rén búyào lànyòng bǎojiànpǐn。
Healthy people shouldn\'t use health products too much.
老总在大会上讲的都是一些浮辞滥调。
Lǎozǒng zài dàhuì shàng jiǎng de dōushì yìxiē fúcí làndiào。
What the boss said at the meeting is a cliche.
医药专家呼吁，伽马刀不可滥用。
Yīyào zhuānjiā hūyù，jiāmǎdāo bùkě lànyòng。
Experts on medicine appeal to the whole world not to misuse the gamma knife.
人类乱砍滥伐，终于酿成了沙尘暴这杯苦酒！
Rénlèi luànkǎn lànfá，zhōng yú niàngchéng le shāchénbào zhè bēi kǔjiǔ！
Man cuts trees at random, finally causing a deplorable consequence --- the sand storm.
你如此滥发广告传单，没有一点针对性，是不会有什么效果的！
Nǐ rúcǐ lànfā guǎnggào chuándān，méiyǒu yìdiǎn zhēnduìxìng，shì búhuì yǒu shénme xiàoguǒ de！
The fly paper will have no effect since you distribute it haphazardly.
这些恶霸如此横行滥杀，早晚是会进监牢的！
Zhèxiē èbà rúcǐ héngxíng lànshā，zǎowǎn shì huì jìn jiānláo de！
Killing innocent people indiscriminately, these local tyrants will be put in prison one day.
《诗经》是中国诗歌滥觞。
《Shījīng》 shì Zhōngguó shīgē lànshāng。
The Book of Poetry is the origin of Chinese poetry.
戏曲这种艺术形式滥觞于宋朝。
Xìqǔ zhèzhǒng yìshù xíngshì lànshāngyú Sòngcháo。
Traditional opera originated in the Song dynasty.
用这些滥套子是解决不了实际问题的。
Yòng zhèxiē làntàozi shì jiějué bùliǎo shíjì wèntí de。
Platitudes can not solve practical problems.

她觉得交朋友应该宁缺勿滥，要交就交个优秀的朋友。

She holds the view that it\'s better not to make friends than to make an unsuitable friend.
我们已经开始着手治理散滥的音像市场了。
wǒmen yǐjing kāishǐ zhuóshǒu zhìlǐ sǎnlàn de yīn xiàng shìchǎng le。
We have already started to control the indiscriminate spread of the audiovisual market.
我们要保护这一带的天然林，严禁乱砍滥伐！
Wǒmen yào bǎohù zhè yídài de tiānránlín，yánjìn luànkǎn lànfá！
We must protect the natural woods here, and strictly forbid the cutting down of trees.
使用下三滥的手段对付朋友的人都是卑鄙小人。
Shǐyòng xiàsānlàn de shǒuduàn duìfù péngyou de rén dōushì bēibǐ xiǎorén。
Those who use dirty tricks against their friends are  disgusting people.
滥用有机肥料可能会导致土地的土质下降。
Lànyòng yǒujī féiliào kěnéng huì dǎozhì tǔdì de tǔzhì xiàjiàng。
Misusing organic fertilizer may cause a decrease in the soil\'s quality.

lànyòng

When buying clothes, I go by the principle of quality over quantity.

Zhèpiān wénzhāng duì guānliáozhǔyì zuòfēng jìnxíngle xīnlà de fěngcì。
This piece is a biting satire on bureaucracy.
官僚
官僚主义危害，甚于水火。
封建官僚
对群众不能耍官僚
官僚主义。
to fight one\'s way through red tape
冲破官僚主义的重重阻碍
He defines bureaucrat as a desk-bound employee.
他把那些坐办公室的人称之为官僚。
The bureaucracy controls the government.
Guānliáozhǔyì kòngzhìle zhèngfǔ。
官僚主义控制了政府。
The problems of inefficient bureaucracies are compounded by poor laws and indifferent enforcement.
Dīxiào guānliáozhǔyì suǒ dàilái de wèntí yóuyú fǎlǜ bù wánshàn yǐjí zhífǎ bù yán ér xiǎnde gèngjiā fùzá。
低效官僚主义所带来的问题由于法律不完善以及执法不严而显得更加复杂。
We need to cut the bureaucracy in higher education.
Wǒmen bìxū xiāochú gāoděng jiàoyù zhōng de guānliáo tèzhēng。
我们必须消除高等教育中的官僚特征。
Long hours are often a reflection of an organization\'s bureaucratic inefficiency.
Bànshì tuōlā jīngcháng shì yí gè zǔzhī jīgòu guānliáozuòfēng yánzhòng、xiàolǜ dīxià de biǎoxiàn。
办事拖拉经常是一个组织机构官僚作风严重、效率低下的表现。
You will find a lot of bureaucracy in this company.
Nǐ huì zài zhège gōngsī kàndào hěn yánzhòng de guānliáo zuòfēng。
你会在这个公司看到很严重的官僚作风。
Bureaucracy is a dirty word and it shouldn\'t be used in our company.
Guānliáozuòfēng shì yí gè lìngrén jìhuì de zìyǎn，bù yīnggāi chūxiàn zài wǒmen gōngsī。
官僚作风是一个另人忌讳的字眼，不应该出现在我们公司。
Red tape has considerably slowed our efficiency.
Guānliáo zhǔyì yánzhòng jiàngdīle wǒmen de xiàolǜ。
官僚主义严重降低了我们的效率。
The Government is trying to promote small businesses and to cut out some of the bureaucracy.
Zhèngfǔ zhèng shìtú tuīguǎng xiǎo qǐyè，qǔxiāo yìxiē guānliáo jīgòu。
政府正试图推广小企业，取消一些官僚机构。
The bureaucracy paralyzes the entire operation.
Guānliáotǐzhì shǐ zhěnggè xíngdòng tānhuàn le。
官僚体制使整个行动瘫痪了。
His bureaucratic behavior annoyed his colleagues.
Tā de guānliáo zuòfēng lìng tā de tóngshìmen fēicháng tǎoyàn。
他的官僚作风令他的同事们非常讨厌。
The choice between bureaucracy and adhocracy represents a common dilemma.
Rúhé zài guānliáo tǐzhì yǔ mínzhǔ zìyóu tǐzhì zhījiān zuòchū xuǎnzé，zhè dàibiǎole yì zhǒng pǔbiàn de jìntuìliǎngnán de kùnjìng。
如何在官僚体制与民主自由体制之间做出选择，这代表了一种普遍的进退两难的困境。
The bureaucrats explained smugly that the facts provided by their own experts show no cause for concern.
Guānliáomen zìmíngdéyì de jiěshì shuō，tāmen zìjǐ de zhuānjiā suǒ tígōng de shìshí biǎomíng méiyǒu shénme hǎo dānxīn de。
官僚们自鸣得意地解释说，他们自己的专家所提供的事实表明没有什么好担心的。
His bureaucratically petty behavior annoyed her.
Tā wúliáo de guānliáo zuòfēng rěnǎole tā。
他无聊的官僚作风惹恼了她。
Technocracy was described as that society in which those who govern justify themselves by appeal to scientific forms of knowledge.
Jìshù guānliáo bèi xíngróng wèi zhǎngwò lǐngdǎo quánlì bìng jùyǒu kēxué zhīshí bèijǐng de yì qún rén。
技术官僚被形容为掌握领导权利并具有科学知识背景的一群人。
Normally the judge and I are allies, equal partners in the justice system.
Tōngcháng shuō，wǒ hé fǎguān shì tóngliáo，wǒmen shì sīfǎ xìtǒng de píngděng hézuò huǒbàn。
通常说，我和法官是同僚，我们是司法系统的平等合作伙伴。
一些美国的阁僚在现场观看NBA比赛。
Yìxiē Měiguó de géliáo zài xiànchǎng guānkàn NBA bǐsài。
Several cabinet officials are watching the NBA games live.
众臣僚坚决反对再次增加百姓的赋税。

我怎么也发不好英语里的复辅音。
Wǒ zěnme yě fā bùhǎo yīngyǔ lǐ de fùfǔyīn。
I can\'t pronounce consonant clusters in English properly.
Russian distinguished between hard consonants and palatalized or soft consonants.
Éyǔ qūfēn yìng fǔyīn hé èhuà fǔyīn huò ruǎn fǔyīn。
俄语区分硬辅音和腭化辅音或软辅音。
This vowel is usually elided before a single consonant.
Zhège yuányīn zài dāngè fǔyīn zìmǔ qián tōngcháng bù fāyīn。
这个元音在单个辅音字母前通常不发音。
a double consonant
双辅音
a lip consonant
唇辅音
p.t.k. etc. are voiceless consonants
p、t、k、等是清辅音
When do you double the final consonant?
在什么情况下双写词尾的辅音字母？
Some of the consonants have a hard sound when you pronounce them.
Yǒuxiē fǔyīn zài fāshēng shí xūyào fā yìng\'èyīn。
有些辅音在发声时需要发硬腭音。
Grimm showed how the consonants shifted.
Gélín jiěshìle fǔyīn rúhé chǎnshēng yīnbiàn。
格林解释了辅音如何产生音变。
The nasal assimilates to the following consonant.
Gāi bíyīn yǔ xiàliè fǔyīn tīng qǐlái xiāngsì。
该鼻音与下列辅音听起来相似。
I worry about the second Germanic consonant shift.
Wǒ duì dì-èr déyǔ fǔyīn yídòng yǒuxiē dānxīn。
我对第二德语辅音移动有些担心。
Indian accents can be characterized by the fact that speakers retroflex their consonants.
Yìndù kǒuyīn de tèzhēng shì，jiǎnghuàrén yòng juǎnshéyīn dú fǔyīn。
印度口音的特征是，讲话人用卷舌音读辅音。
Between two consonants, this liquid is vowelized.
Zài liǎng gè fǔyīn zhījiān，zhège liúyīn yuányīnhuà le。
在两个辅音之间，这个流音元音化了。
This consonant always occurs medially.
Zhège fǔyīn zìmǔ zǒngshì chūxiàn zài zhōngjiān。
这个辅音字母总是出现在中间。
The consonants are geminated in these words.
Fǔyīn zài zhèxiē dāncí zhōng dōuyào shuāngxiě。
辅音在这些单词中都要双写。
These consonants dissimilate.
Zhèxiē fǔyīn bù xiāngtóng。
这些辅音不相同。
The consonant reduplicates after a short vowel.
Duǎn yuányīn zhīhòu de fǔyīn yào shuāngxiě。
短元音之后的辅音要双写。
His stop consonants are too aspirated.
Tā de bìsè fǔyīn guòyú fā chéng sòngqì yīn le。
他的闭塞辅音过于发成送气音了。
以自力更生为主，外援为辅
yǐ zìlìgèngshēngwéi zhǔ，wàiyuán wéi fǔ 
rely mainly on one\'s own efforts while making external assistance subsidiary
Volunteers could supplement but could not be substituted for regular employees.
Zhìyuànzhě kěyǐ fǔzhù，dàn bùnéng dàitì zhèngshì yuángōng。

too late to repent
